< Text>
I recently had hand surgery at Fresno Surgical Hospital and based on the experience I had, I felt it imperative to leave a review. I am extremely nervous when it comes to surgery and anesthesia, because I usually get very ill postoperatively.

The entire staff took great care of me and kept me pretty calm through the entire process. I'm very happy to report that I did not get sick postoperatively. From my surgeon to the anesthesiologist and nursing staff, I received excellent care. I only wish I could recall my surgical team's names, because they were exceptional. Postoperative staff were also fantastic! Truly the best surgical experience I've ever had. I also received a get well soon card in the mail with staff's handwritten notes. I most definitely would recommend anyone having surgery to have it at this hospital.

Thank you for the exceptional care Fresno Surgical!!</Text>

I WOULD have given a 5 star review, but alas, just yesterday I received the DRIEST, most OVERCOOKED cheese steak sandwich, the large, which is a $22 sandwich, all that with no bell peppers in it.
Granted, the BOBBIE is one of the most delicious sandwiches EVER, the cheese steak is USUALLY SUPER DUPER, but the meatball sandwich was mediocre at best.
Shame on Capriottis, I mean Subway, because a TWENTY DOLLAR SANDWICH should NEVER be dry or lacking. C'mon already. It's a SANDWICH.

Essentially, Capriottis is everything that subway isn't, deliciously soft and chewy bread, but really, who can eat bread these days anyway.
Capriottis is Subway but OPPOSITE, while the latter has Jared as a spokesperson touting a regemin of healthy lifestyle choices, Capriottis spokesperson would probably be more like The Godfather, totally unconcerned with fitness or diet, as the Bobbie stacks bread with more bread, deliciously sinful and forcing extra workout days in between.

Sounds like there are several things that you are not pleased with and I want to address all of them.  When it comes to the music, UFC Gym Radio is a podcast that has a mixture of genres - House, dub Step, rap, rock, and a little bit of pop.  The mixes are anywhere from 1.5 hours to 2 hours long, therefore skipping songs is a little difficult to do.  When it comes to turning down the volume, it is all contingent upon the time of the day.  If it is during any of the busy times of the gym, we keep the volume up to help support the classes.  However, I do see that you workout very early in the morning.  The reason that it is not able to be turned down is because only management has access to the music/sound/volume room, therefor the front desk associate would not be able to accommodate.  I will work on making sure that the volume is turned down during the slower hours of the gym, but we do encourage that people do not wear head phones; as it creates a better sense of community in the gym.\n\nWhen it comes to the normal weight lifting machines, I am sorry you feel that way.  We have several machine weights, yes they might not be considered normal, but they are the latest model of the machines.  We have 25 machines, 2 leg press (1 dual action), 6 squat racks, 4 Olympic lifting stations, 19 station cable machine, 2 smith machines (1 dual action), 6 flat benches, 9 hammer strength machines, and dumbbells ranging from 5 - 120 lbs (2 sets).  In addition to this, we have a Hex bar, 10 extra bars for dead lifts, and miscellaneous exercises, and plenty of other toys to play with upstairs.  Our focus here at the UFC gym is that everyone works with a coach either privately or in a class.  Therefore, if you see something missing or are not familiar with, we have plenty of people that help take your exercises to the next level.\n\nPutting weights back is something that we encourage our members to do in addition to the staff, as do all gyms.  We do have our special operations team there at night to help aid in the re-racking of weights but we are definitely not perfect and can improve upon that.  Unfortunately at 3:00am, you are correct that we do not have team cleans but during the hours of 7:00am - 10:00pm it is required that our coaches, operations, and membership team do a team clean.  In between the hours of 3:00am - 7:00am we do not have our special operations team on staff, as this is the slowest time of the gym.  But, perception is everything - if you say it never gets cleaned, we need to improve (as we always can).\n\nWhen it comes to the things you mention upstairs, we are very casual here with gym bags, towels, and personal belongings.  While people are in classes and/or working out, they are allowed to bring their stuff with them - most Martial Arts participants can have anything from Extra clothes, hand wraps, gloves, Gi's rash guards, mouth pieces, water bottles, pre-workout, etc.  With this, comes leaving a water bottle or two around and towels not put in the bins - we will improve on this.\n\nOnce again - tank you for taking the time to write this review. Ola has incredible Mexican food, tasty drinks and is in a great location over looking the Long Beach harbor.

I ordered the lobster tacos which were amazing, a margarita, guac & the street corn. It was quite pricey so I have yet to go back, but if it were a bit more reasonable you bet I would be back way more frequently. The service is fine, nothing special but not bad either.

Definitely make a reservation or you will have to wait awhile for a table. I haven't been since before covid times so I am not sure how they are adhering to CDC recommendations (masks, social distancing, etc).

Great spot for a special event! Enjoy :)<//Review>

<Rate>4< /Rate>< Review>
Great concept and delicious Mac and cheese. I tried the shells with broccoli, bacon and mushrooms all topped with hot cheetos..which was a fun experience. If I had to do it again I'd pick a different crunchy topping or have them add less, because the cheetos overwhelmed the other flavors. Also, a highlight was getting the Mexican Coca-Cola in the bottle...delicious. I built my own but could see trying one of the pasta mixes on the menu as well. These would be good if you don't want to make decisions and just want a pre-set mix. Great outdoor seating area and good location at sunset considering how chilly S.F. can get.

Be aware that this Russian Hill area has lots of restaurants and parking can be difficult. All in all and fun place to eat at, and area to be in.< /Review>

<UserId.>111496691757497788146</UserId.><name>Caliboi J< /name><time>1599356353917<//time><Rating>5< /Rating>< review>
San Franciscans‚Äô, though I am not a native of your city, I do have respect for a great number of the eateries this city has to offer.  With the continuation of COVID-19 restrictions, I have been searching for good food, fair prices, delivery ‚Äúon-time‚Äù, etc., and discovered I was only able to get one of the 3 or a combination thereof.   Today, I found MAC‚ÄôD, delivered by Cavier (DoorDash).

‚ÄòMichelin‚Äô rated they are not ‚Äì but they should be and I don‚Äôt mean a one-star rating!  (Note: San Francisco is home to about 36 Michelin Star Restaurants, most one-star rated).  I lived in SOMA and the restaurant I ordered from was located at 2127 Polk St (about a 10-minute drive from me.  I ordered the Hellapeno (w/ jalapenos, roasted mushrooms and chicken) and Mac‚Äôd Wings (BBQ and Buffalo).  Under special instructions, I noted that I was a fan of heat and to turn it up!  They did not disappoint!  The pasta was cooked to perfection with just the right amount of sauce and cheese.  It was rich and creamy ‚Äì smooth.  The additions set it off!  The meal was properly packaged to hold the heat.  I shared this with a friend and really understanding what a mistake I made.  The wings, as far as I‚Äôm concerned, were by far better that any wing I‚Äôve ever had and yes, they did turn up the heat!  And I‚Äôm referring to Wing Stop and Buffalo Wild Wings!

It took approximately 35 minutes from the time I placed my order until it actually arrived.  I‚Äôm not sure what my expectations were BUT this I do know ‚Ä¶. My food arrived HOT.  Not warm.  HOT!  That in itself was worth the price of admission.  The flavors and textures took me back to a period in time were pride was taken in the kitchens of restaurants as they compete for customers in the city that is known for loyalty to the only the absolute BEST.  I was shocked and amazed at the same time and to think that I had all be given up on being completely satisfied conducting a transaction.  Thank you, Mac‚Äôd.

This was a great experience.  The quality of the food, the portions, their packaging and the price.  I got a damn good meal at a fair price; delivered safely and done so with pride.  If this is the service I can expect every time I place an order ‚Äì trust and believe I will be ordering at least 5 days a week.

To the kitchen staff I have this to say:  YOU GUYS ROCK!  I have not had food this well prepared and packaged for delivery in more than 2 years!  Thank you for a job well done!  To the owners:  You have some  amazing recipes.  If you ever become a rated restaurant I fear that it may push your operations beyond anything you can imagine.  I am a person big on ‚Äúservice‚Äù and ‚Äúsatisfaction‚Äù both of which your place not only met but exceeded my expectations.  Again, thank you.< /review>

< text>
Macaroni and cheese is such a simple meal, but Mac'D elevates it by providing multiple choices and cheeses to enhance your experience. Each of us got a different meal, and each came away overjoyed. The kids said that the wings were cooked perfectly, and the French fries were hot and seasoned perfectly, but the real star was the mac and cheese. I got the Hellapeno sauce, which provided a slight kick of heat, which went perfectly with the beef chorizo that is chose as my topper. See, the majority of add-ons are free, and you can get anything from mushrooms to Flaming hot Cheetos on your meal.

You can't go wrong here, and you gotta try it at least once.</text>

<Review>Decent theater with decent screens and decent service. It is pretty clean, which I definitely appreciate. I feel like it could really step up its game, though - many theaters I've gone to in recent years have a LOT more concession stand options. Here, if you want food, they pretty much just have popcorn, hot dogs, "nachos" (just a bag of chips with liquid cheese, no other topping options) and candy. Don't come to a movie hungry, haha.
